<script>
		function get_calling_code(country , form , id)
		{	
			if(country == "")
			{
				return;
			}
			$.ajax({
				type: "POST",
				url: "/signup/get_country_code",
				data: "country_id="+country,
				dataType: "html",
				beforeSend: function() {
					$("#county_loading_code").show();
				},
				complete: function() {
					$("#county_loading_code").hide();
				},
				success: function(msg)
				{
					$("#"+form+" #"+id).val("+"+msg);
				}
			});
		}
		</script>
</div>

</span>

<script>
		function get_calling_code(country , form , id)
		{	
			if(country == "")
			{
				return;
			}
			$.ajax({
				type: "POST",
				url: "/signup/get_country_code",
				data: "country_id="+country,
				dataType: "html",
				beforeSend: function() {
					$("#county_loading_code").show();
				},
				complete: function() {
					$("#county_loading_code").hide();
				},
				success: function(msg)
				{
					$("#"+form+" #"+id).val("+"+msg);

		}
		</script>

<script>
		function get_calling_code(country , form , id)
		{	
			if(country == "")
			{
				return;
			}
			$.ajax({
				type: "POST",
				url: "/signup/get_country_code",
				data: "country_id="+country,
				dataType: "html",
				beforeSend: function() {
					$("#county_loading_code").show();
				},
				complete: function() {
					$("#county_loading_code").hide();
				},
				success: function(msg)
				{
					$("#"+form+" #"+id).val("+"+msg);
				}
			});
		}
		</script>

<script>
		function get_calling_code(country , form , id)
		{	
			if(country == "")
			{
				return;
			}
			$.ajax({
				type: "POST",
				url: "/signup/get_country_code",
				data: "country_id="+country,
				dataType: "html",
				beforeSend: function() {
					$("#county_loading_code").show();
				},
				complete: function() {
					$("#county_loading_code").hide();
				},
				success: function(msg)
				{
					$("#"+form+" #"+id).val("+"+msg);
				}
			});
		}
		</script>

<script>
		function get_calling_code(country , form , id)
		{	
			if(country == "")
			{
				return;
			}
			$.ajax({
				type: "POST",
				url: "/signup/get_country_code",
				data: "country_id="+country,
				dataType: "html",
				beforeSend: function() {
					$("#county_loading_code").show();
				},
				complete: function() {
					$("#county_loading_code").hide();
				},
				success: function(msg)
				{
					$("#"+form+" #"+id).val("+"+msg);
				}
			});
		}
		</script>

<script>
		function get_calling_code(country , form , id)
		{	
			if(country == "")
			{
				return;
			}
			$.ajax({
				type: "POST",
				url: "/signup/get_country_code",
				data: "country_id="+country,
				dataType: "html",
				beforeSend: function() {
					$("#county_loading_code").show();
				},
				complete: function() {
					$("#county_loading_code").hide();
				},
				success: function(msg)
				{
					$("#"+form+" #"+id).val("+"+msg);
				}
			});
		}
		</script>

<script>
function verfiy_email_exit(email , forms , div)
{
	if(email == "")
	{
		return;
	}

	$.ajax({
		type: "POST",
		url: "/tools/signup_verify_email",
		data: "email="+email,
		dataType: "json",
		beforeSend: function() {
			$("#"+forms+ " "+ "#loading" ).text("Loading").show();
		},
		complete: function() {
			$("#"+forms+ " "+ "#loading" ).text('').hide();
		},
		success: function(msg)
		{	
			if(msg.msg != 1)
			{
				$("#"+forms+ " "+ "#"+div).text(msg.msg).show();
			}
			else if(msg.msg == 1)
			{
				$("#"+forms+ " "+ "#"+div).text("").hide();
			}
		}
	});	
}
function redirecttopaypage() {
	var xhttp = new XMLHttpRequest();
	xhttp.onreadystatechange = function() {
		if (this.readyState == 4 && this.status == 200) {
			window.open(this.response);
		}
	};
	xhttp.open("POST", "https://www.exporthub.com/redirecttopaypage", true);
	xhttp.setRequestHeader("Content-type", "application/x-www-form-urlencoded");
	xhttp.send('_token="Y2Huwz9vyuJYphYTMjNxlsqWnBUJxsTQiWcTnK1s"');
}

<script>

	var d = new Date();
	var n = d.getTimezoneOffset();
	var result = (n/60) * -1;
	setCookie("time_zone" , result , 365);
	function setCookie(cname, cvalue, exdays) {
	  var d = new Date();
	  d.setTime(d.getTime() + (exdays*24*60*60*1000));
	  var expires = "expires="+ d.toUTCString();
	  document.cookie = cname + "=" + cvalue + ";" + expires + ";path=/";
	}

<p class="intro-cnt J-txt-cnt">
		Cardy Intelligent Technology Co.Limited, founded in 2004 as a private-owned ordinary tax payer is located in NanShan District of ShenZhen where many high-tech enterprises centralized, and its registered trademark is KD. and ã€‚Since established, we have been trying efforts to use the most advanced technology to create high quality brand, and win customers via quality and humanized service. We always abide by the theory of talent strengthens enterprise, and absorb a large number of outstanding talents to our company. It is renowned for strictness and efficiency on management. Company relies on quality to win competition, technology to develop market, service to satisfy customers€ as management theory. We provide customers qualified products and best service via first grade technology and rich experience. ã€‚Its products contain contact and non-contact IC Cardy and RFID tag product (low frequency, high frequency, super high frequency), it is a professional manufacturer focusing on producing integrated circuit Cardy and electric tag products. It has advanced national and international production lines like bonding, coil winding, printing, layer pressing and capsulation, meanwhile it is equipped with various auxiliary business including subsequent coding, programming and input of customer€™s data, COS development, personalized proposal, etc. It has the experience on large scale projects on multiple high-way, city public traffic and university, etc. and matured oversea project cooperated resolutions. With rich experience, it keeps more completed cooperation relations with national several system merchants. Time and different requirements of different customers create and accumulate rich experience for Cardy production, meanwhile the development course from non to have, from small to big remind Cardy maker timely: consciousness should be advanced and product quality should be stable, staff quality should be high, then company can survive.At present, Cardy business network spread all over the country, with the active promotion on RFID product application on various industries all over the world, the demand on RFID product is increasing. The product is widely used on public traffic, speedway, campus, telecom, and internet bar, supermarket, transportation, consumption and safety and identification circles. Based on the principle of surviving on quality, developing on credit and technical innovation as basis, it walks on the front of the circle and keeps trying to satisfy the different requirements of market. Cardy maker is expecting to develop and create prosperity with all of users.
        </p>

<script>
		function get_calling_code(country , form , id)
		{	
			if(country == "")
			{
				return;
			}
			$.ajax({
				type: "POST",
				url: "/signup/get_country_code",
				data: "country_id="+country,
				dataType: "html",
				beforeSend: function() {
					$("#county_loading_code").show();
				},
				complete: function() {
					$("#county_loading_code").hide();
				},
				success: function(msg)
				{
					$("#"+form+" #"+id).val("+"+msg);
				}
			});
		}
		</script>
</div>
</div>

<script>
		function get_calling_code(country , form , id)
		{	
			if(country == "")
			{
				return;
			}
			$.ajax({
				type: "POST",
				url: "/signup/get_country_code",
				data: "country_id="+country,
				dataType: "html",
				beforeSend: function() {
					$("#county_loading_code").show();
				},
				complete: function() {
					$("#county_loading_code").hide();
				},
				success: function(msg)
				{
					$("#"+form+" #"+id).val("+"+msg);
				}
			});
		}
		</script>

            function verfiy_email_exit(email , forms , div)
            {
                if(email == "")
                {
                    return;
                }

                $.ajax({
                    type: "POST",
                    url: "/tools/signup_verify_email",
                    data: "email="+email,
                    dataType: "json",
                    success: function(msg)
                    {
                        if(msg.msg != 1)
                        {
                            $("#"+forms+ " "+ "#"+div).text(msg.msg).show();
                        }
                        else if(msg.msg == 1)
                        {
                            $("#"+forms+ " "+ "#"+div).text("").hide();
                        }
                    }
                });
            }

            });

<script>
		function get_calling_code(country , form , id)
		{	
			if(country == "")
			{
				return;
			}
			$.ajax({
				type: "POST",
				url: "/signup/get_country_code",
				data: "country_id="+country,
				dataType: "html",
				beforeSend: function() {
					$("#county_loading_code").show();
				},
				complete: function() {
					$("#county_loading_code").hide();
				},
				success: function(msg)
				{
					$("#"+form+" #"+id).val("+"+msg);
				}
			});
		}
		</script>

		function verfiy_email_exit(email , forms , div)
		{
			if(email == "")
			{
				return;
			}

			$.ajax({
				type: "POST",
				url: "/tools/signup_verify_email",
				data: "email="+email,
				dataType: "json",
				success: function(msg)
				{
					if(msg.msg != 1)
					{
						$("#"+forms+ " "+ "#"+div).text(msg.msg).show();
					}
					else if(msg.msg == 1)
					{
						$("#"+forms+ " "+ "#"+div).text("").hide();
					}
				}
			});
		}

<script type="text/javascript">
    function isNumberKey(evt)   {
            var e = evt || window.event; //window.event is safer, thanks @ThiefMaster
            var charCode = e.which || e.keyCode;
            if (charCode > 31 && (charCode < 47 || charCode > 57))
             return false;
             if (e.shiftKey) return false;
            return true;
         }
        $("#toggle_sCartitmesBig_mobts_kwd").click(function() {
           var elem = $("#toggle_sCartitmesBig_mobts_kwd").text();
           if (elem == "Show More +") {
                //Stuff to do when btn is in the read more state
                $("#toggle_sCartitmesBig_mobts_kwd").text("Show Less -");
               $(".content_sCartitmesBig_mobts_kwd").slideDown();
        } else {
               //Stuff to do when btn is in the read less state
               $("#toggle_sCartitmesBig_mobts_kwd").text("Show More +");
              $(".content_sCartitmesBig_mobts_kwd").slideUp();       }


        });
    function set_buyer() {
       $("#is_buyer_seller").val(1);
        var PreselectedCountryID = $('#eh_company_contact_form #PreselectedCountryID').val();
        var PreselectedCountryID1 = $('#eh_company_contact_form #country_offcompanies').val();

    function get_city_names_from_signup(){
        var token =$('#token_signup_page_cities').val();
        var country_id = $('#country_offcompanies').val();

        var search_str = "&_token="+token+"&country_id="+country_id;

        req = $.ajax({
        async:true,
            type:'POST',
            url:'/signup/get_cities_names_signup',
            data: search_str,
            success: function(e){
                $('#city_offcompanies').html(e);
                $('.selectpicker').selectpicker('refresh');

            }
        });
    }

        submitHandler: function (validator, form, submitButton) {

                var email = $('#email').val();
                var token = $('#signup_token').val();

                // Confirm Email Address
                $.ajax({
                    type: "POST",
                    url: "/tools/signup_verify_email",
                    data: $('#eh_company_contact_form').serialize(),
                    dataType: "json",
                    async:true,
                    success: function (res) {
                        if(res.msg != 1){
                            $('#email_exists').show();
                            $('#form_success').hide();
                        }else{
                            $('#email_exists').hide();
                            //$('#lodingoverlay_signuppage').show();
                            $.ajax({
                                async:true,
                                type: 'POST',
                                url: '/signup/submit_widget',
                                data:$('#eh_company_contact_form').serialize()+"&page_url="+$("link[rel='canonical']").attr("href"),
                                success: function (msg) {
                                        var return_msg = $.parseJSON(msg);
                                        //alert(return_msg);
                                        if(return_msg!=5) {
                                            //$('#lodingoverlay_signuppage').hide();
                                            $('#form_success').show();
                                            $('#email_exists').hide();
                                            $('#CaptchaError').hide();
                                            $('#eh_company_contact_form .form-group').removeClass('has-success');
                                            $('#eh_company_contact_form .form-group').removeClass('has-error');
                                            $('#eh_company_contact_form')[0].reset();
                                            // five parameters, send, hitType, eventCategory, eventAction, eventLabel
                                            send_popup_signup('send', 'event', 'Signups', 'Signup', 'offcompany_signup');
                                            setTimeout(function () {
                                                location.reload();
                                            }, 3000);
                                        }
                                        else if(return_msg==5)
                                        {
                                            $('#form_success').hide();
                                            $('#email_exists').hide();
                                            $('#CaptchaError').show();
                                            setTimeout(function () {
                                                $('#CaptchaError').hide();
                                            }, 3000);

                                        }
                                    }
                                });
                        }
                    }
                });
            }





     }, // Submit Handler

    // Remove the spaces from the entered and generated code
    function removeSpaces(string){
        return string.split(' ').join('');
    }


    function claim_method_off()    {
        //$('#claim_submit_button').attr('disabled','disabled');
        var form_data = $("#claim_company_form");
        var data = form_data.serialize();
        document.getElementById("error-list-supplier").innerHTML = "";
        //var captcha = checkform();
        errors=0;
        /*if(captcha === false)    {
            errors=1;
        }*/
        if($("#claim_mobile").val() == '')
        {
            errors=1;
            document.getElementById("claim_mobile").style.border="3px solid red";
        }
        else
        {
            document.getElementById("claim_mobile").style.border="1px solid #ccc";
        }

        if($("#claim_name").val() == '')
        {
            errors=1;
            document.getElementById("claim_name").style.border="3px solid red";
        }
        else
        {
            document.getElementById("claim_name").style.border="1px solid #ccc";
        }

        if($("#claim_email").val() == '')
        {
            errors=1;
            document.getElementById("claim_email").style.border="3px solid red";
        }
        else
        {
            var validate_email = ValidateEmail($("#claim_email").val());
            if(validate_email){
                document.getElementById("claim_email").style.border="1px solid #ccc";
            }else{
                errors=1;
                document.getElementById("claim_email").style.border="3px solid red";
            }
        }

        if($("#captcha_occ").length>0)
        {
            if ($("#captcha_occ").val() == '') {
                errors = 1;
                document.getElementById("captcha_occ").style.border = "3px solid red";
            } else {
                document.getElementById("captcha_occ").style.border = "1px solid #ccc";
            }
        }


        if(errors == 1)
        {
            return false;
        }
        $('#claim_submit_button').attr('disabled','disabled');

        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
                url: "/claim_your_company_off",
            data:data,
            success: function (get_data) {
                if (get_data.data.status=='1') {
                    $('.error-list-claim').hide();
                    $('.success-message-claim').show();
                    setTimeout(function () {
                        $('.success-message-claim').fadeOut();
                        $('#claim_popup').modal('hide');
                    }, 3000);
                }else if(get_data.data.status=='2')
                {
                    $('.error-list-claim').hide();
                    $('.success-message-claim').hide();
                    $('.error-list-claim2').show();
                    $('.error-list-claim2').html(get_data.data.message);
                    setTimeout(function () {
                        $('.error-list-claim2').fadeOut();
                        //$('#claim_popup').modal('hide');
                    }, 3000);

                }else {
                    $('.success-message-claim').hide();
                    $('.error-list-claim').show();
                    $('.error-list-claim2').hide();
                    $('.error-list-claim').html(get_data.data.message);
                    //$('#claim_submit_button').removeAttr('disabled');
                    setTimeout(function() {
                        $('.error-list-claim').fadeOut();
                        //$('#claim_popup').modal('hide');
                    }, 3000);
                }
                //console.log(get_data.data.message);
                $('#claim_submit_button').removeAttr('disabled');
            }
        });
    }

	function verfiy_email_exit(email , forms , div)
	{
		if(email == "")
		{
			return;
		}

		$.ajax({
			type: "POST",
			url: "/tools/signup_verify_email",
			data: "email="+email,
			dataType: "json",
			success: function(msg)
			{	
				if(msg.msg != 1)
				{
					$("#"+forms+ " "+ "#"+div).text(msg.msg).show();
				}
				else if(msg.msg == 1)
				{
					$("#"+forms+ " "+ "#"+div).text("").hide();
				}
			}
		});	
	}

                    $(this).closest('p').find('span').fadeIn('slow').show();

            function get_cookie(Name) {
                var Name = Name + "=";
                var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
                for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
                    var c = ca[i];
                    while (c.charAt(0) == ' ')c = c.substring(1, c.length);
                    if (c.indexOf(Name) == 0)return unescape(c.substring(Name.length, c.length));
                }
                return "";

            }



            var site_id = '1';
            var login = '';
            var kwd = 'smart card(contact, contactless) , rfid card,';

            var available;
            var percentage_of_page;
            var half_screen;
            var height;

            $(window).scroll(function (e) {
                available = $(document).height();
                percentage_of_page = 0.01;
                half_screen = available * percentage_of_page;
                height = $(window).scrollTop();
                if ( height > half_screen ) {
                    if((site_id == 2 || site_id == 4) && (login == '') &&(getCookie('mem_info')) != 3 )
                    {
                        view_member_info(kwd,'off company',' Provide Your Details to View Complete Results');
                    }
                }
            });

<script type="text/javascript">
	$(document).ready(function(){
		var elm_class = '.scroll_top_new';
		$(window).scroll(function(){
			if ($(this).scrollTop() > 300) {
				$(elm_class).show();
			} else {
				$(elm_class).hide();
			}
		});
		$(elm_class).click(function(){
			$('html, body').animate({scrollTop : 0},800);
			return false;
		});
	});
</script>

	function close_connect_representative()
	{
		var expires = "";
		var days = 365;
		var name = '_cwtr';
		var value = 1;
		if (days) {
			var date = new Date();
			date.setTime(date.getTime() + (days*24*60*60*1000));
			expires = "; expires=" + date.toUTCString();
		}
		document.cookie = name + "=" + (value || "")  + expires + "; path=/";
	}
	
	function getcookies(name) {
	   var nameEQ = name + "=";
		var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
		for(var i=0;i < ca.length;i++) {
			var c = ca[i];
			while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1,c.length);
			if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length,c.length);
		}
		return false;
	}

    function keyupFunction() {
        var x = document.getElementById("buyer_selling_products_idpd").value;
        var element  = document.getElementById('erro_buyer_selling_products_pd');
        if(x!=''){
            document.getElementById("erro_buyer_selling_products_pd").style.display = "none";
        }else{
            document.getElementById("erro_buyer_selling_products_pd").style.display = "block";
        }
    }

    /*************************** Refresh CSRF Token Code Start *****************************/
    function get_token() {
        var token = 'Y2Huwz9vyuJYphYTMjNxlsqWnBUJxsTQiWcTnK1s';
        var config_url =$('#config_source_url').val();
        $.ajax({
            headers: {
                'X-CSRF-TOKEN': $('meta[name="csrf-token"]').attr('content')
            },
            data: {_token: 'Y2Huwz9vyuJYphYTMjNxlsqWnBUJxsTQiWcTnK1s'},
            url: "/signup/refreshToken",
            type: "POST",
            dataType: 'json',
            success: function (result) {
                // $('meta[name="csrf-token"]').attr('content', result.token);
                $('#logic_token').val(result.token);
            },
            error: function (xhr, status, error) {
                console.log(xhr);
            }
        });
    }

    /*************************** Refresh CSRF Token Code End *****************************/

    function get_countries_and_code_preselected() {
        var e = $('meta[name="csrf-token"]').attr('content');
        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            url: "/signup/get_country_and_code_for_ajax_call",
            data: {"_token": "Y2Huwz9vyuJYphYTMjNxlsqWnBUJxsTQiWcTnK1s"},
            success: function (get_data) {
                if (get_data!=''){
                    var data = $.parseJSON(get_data);
                    $('.class_for_countries').html(data.all_countries);
                    $('.class_for_code').val(data.country_phone_code);
                }
            },
            complete: function(){
                $('.class_for_countries').selectpicker('refresh');
            }
        });
    }

    function get_country_code_gernalize_new(country_id,drop_down_id){
        //var new_token = {"_token": "Y2Huwz9vyuJYphYTMjNxlsqWnBUJxsTQiWcTnK1s"};

                    if(msg != ""){
                        $('.'+drop_down_id).val(msg.country_code);
                    }
                }
            });
        }
    }

    function setCookie(name,value,hours) {
        var expires = "";
        if (hours) {
            var date = new Date();
            date.setTime(date.getTime() + (hours*60*60*1000));
            expires = "; expires=" + date.toUTCString();
        }
        document.cookie = name + "=" + (value || "")  + expires + "; path=/ ;domain=.exporthub.com";
    }

    function getCookie(name) {
        var nameEQ = name + "=";
        var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
        for(var i=0;i < ca.length;i++) {
            var c = ca[i];
            while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1,c.length);
            if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length,c.length);
        }
        return null;
    }


    function refresh_select_by_id(id) {
        $('#' + id).selectpicker("refresh");
    }

    function refresh_select_by_class(clas) {
        $('.' + clas).selectpicker("refresh");
    }

    /* From Logics */
    function get_countries_logics(seat_id) {

        var e = 'Y2Huwz9vyuJYphYTMjNxlsqWnBUJxsTQiWcTnK1s';
        var con = $('#pre_selected_country').val();
        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            url: "/signup/get_countries",
            data: "_token=" + e+"&country="+con,
            success: function(e) {

                null != $("#" + seat_id) && ($("#" + seat_id).html(e));
                $("#" + seat_id).selectpicker('refresh');
                if(con>0) {
                    if (seat_id != 'cchp_country' || seat_id != 'cchp_country2') {
                        $("#" + seat_id).val(con);
                    } else if (seat_id == 'exit_intent_company') {
                        $("#" + seat_id).html();
                        $("#" + seat_id).html(e);
                    } else {

                        $("#" + seat_id).selectpicker('refresh');
                        $("#" + seat_id).val(con);
                        $('#' + seat_id).selectpicker('refresh');
                    }
                }else{
                    $("#" + seat_id).selectpicker('refresh');
                }

            }
        })
    }

    function get_countries_logics2(seat_id) {

        var e = 'Y2Huwz9vyuJYphYTMjNxlsqWnBUJxsTQiWcTnK1s';
        var con = $('#pre_selected_country').val();
        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            url: "/signup/get_countries",
            data: "_token=" + e,
            success: function(e) {
                null != $("#" + seat_id) && ($("#" + seat_id).html(e));
                if(seat_id==='country_id_desktop'){
                    $("#" + seat_id).selectpicker('refresh');
                }

            }
        })
    }

    function get_country_code_logics(con_id=0){
        var country_id = $('.sidebar_country_generalize').val();

        if(con_id>0){
            country_id= con_id;
        }else {
            if (country_id == "") {
                country_id = $('#pre_selected_country').val();
            }
        }
        var search_str_code = "&country_id="+country_id;
        req = $.ajax({
            async:true,
            type:'POST',
            url:'/signup/get_country_code_flag',
            data: {"_token": "Y2Huwz9vyuJYphYTMjNxlsqWnBUJxsTQiWcTnK1s"}+search_str_code,
            success: function(msg){
                var msg = $.parseJSON(msg);
                if(msg != ""){
                    $('.mcode_loaded').val(msg.country_code);
                }
            }
        });
    }

    function get_city_names(id) {
        var e = "&_token=" + $('#logic_token').val(); + "&country_id=" +id;
        req = $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            url: "/companies/get_cities_names",
            data: e,
            success: function(e) {
                (ht = "") != e && (document.getElementById("cc_city").innerHTML = e, refresh_select("cc_city"))
            }
        });
    }

    function get_country_code_for_side_bar_form(country_seleted_id) {
        var e = "&country_id=" + country_seleted_id;
        req = $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            url: "/signup/get_country_code",
            data: {"_token": "Y2Huwz9vyuJYphYTMjNxlsqWnBUJxsTQiWcTnK1s"}+e,
            success: function(e) {
                $("#phone_no_country_code").val(e);
                $("#mobile_no_country_code").val(e);
            }
        })
    }

        function getUrlVars()

            var vars = [], hash,comp_url;
            var query_string = window.location.href.slice(window.location.href.indexOf('?') + 1).split('&');

        $(".CheckFormat").keydown(function (e) {
            // Allow: backspace, delete, tab, escape, enter and .
            if ($.inArray(e.keyCode, [46, 8, 9, 27, 13, 110, 190]) !== -1 ||
                // Allow: Ctrl/cmd+A
                (e.keyCode == 65 && (e.ctrlKey === true || e.metaKey === true)) ||
                // Allow: Ctrl/cmd+C
                (e.keyCode == 67 && (e.ctrlKey === true || e.metaKey === true)) ||
                // Allow: Ctrl/cmd+X
                (e.keyCode == 88 && (e.ctrlKey === true || e.metaKey === true)) ||
                // Allow: home, end, left, right
                (e.keyCode >= 35 && e.keyCode <= 39)) {
                // let it happen, don't do anything
                return;
            }
            // Ensure that it is a number and stop the keypress
            if ((e.shiftKey || (e.keyCode < 48 || e.keyCode > 57)) && (e.keyCode < 96 || e.keyCode > 105)) {
                e.preventDefault();
            }
        });
        //

        $("form[name='freeconsultancy_supplier']").validate({

        $("#freeconsultancysupplier :submit").click(function (e) {
            var FormCode = $('#FormCodeSupplier').val();
            var FormEnteredCode = $('#FormEnteredCodeSupplier').val();
            if(FormCode==FormEnteredCode) {
                $('#captcha-error-supplier').hide();
            }else{

        });

        $('#FormEnteredCodeSupplier').on("blur",function(){

                $('#captcha-error-supplier').hide();
            }else{

            }
        });

        function Send_data_supplier(data) {
            $.ajax({
                type: "POST",
                url: "https://www.exporthub.com/home/send_consultancy_detail",
                data:data,
                success: function (msg) {
                    if(msg.status == 1)	{
                        $('#success-message-supplier').html(msg.message);
                        setTimeout(function(){location.replace('/member/dashboard?msg=signup-success')}, 3000);
                    }else	{
                        $('#error-list-supplier').html(msg.msg);
                    }
                },
                error: function () {
                },
                complete: function () {
                    $('#success-message-supplier').html('<span>Your Message Has Been Sent Thank you!</span>');
                    setTimeout(function(){location.replace('/member/dashboard?msg=signup-success')}, 3000);
                }
            });
        }

        $("form[name='freeconsultancy_buyer']").validate({
            rules: {
                title: { required: true, maxlength: 100 },
                email: { required: true, email: true, maxlength: 100 },
                mobile: { required: true, maxlength: 15 },
                selling_buying_products: { required: true},
                country: { required: true}
            },
            messages: {
            },
            errorPlacement: function(error, element) {
                element.closest(".input-group").after(error);
            },
            // Make sure the form is submitted to the destination defined
            // in the "action" attribute of the form when valid
            submitHandler: function(form) {
                var form_data = $("#freeconsultancybuyer").find("form");
                var data = form_data.serialize();
                Send_data_buyer(data);
            }
        });

        var FormCode = $('#FormCodeBuyer').val();
        $('#CaptchaCodeBuyer').html(FormCode);

        $("#freeconsultancybuyer :submit").click(function (e) {
            var FormCode = $('#FormCodeBuyer').val();
            var FormEnteredCode = $('#FormEnteredCodeBuyer').val();
            if(FormCode==FormEnteredCode) {
                $('#captcha-error-buyer').hide();
            }else{
                $('#captcha-error-buyer').show();
                e.preventDefault();
            }
        });

        $('#FormEnteredCodeBuyer').on("blur",function(){
            var FormCode = $('#FormCodeBuyer').val();
            var FormEnteredCode = $('#FormEnteredCodeBuyer').val();
            if(FormCode==FormEnteredCode) {
                $('#captcha-error-buyer').hide();
            }else{
                $('#captcha-error-buyer').show();
            }
        });

        function Send_data_buyer(data) {
            $.ajax({
                type: "POST",
                url: "https://www.exporthub.com/home/send_buyer_form",
                data:data,
                dataType: "json",
                success: function (msg) {
                    if(msg.status == 1)	{
                        $('#success-message-buyer').html(msg.message);
                        setTimeout(function(){location.reload()}, 3000);
                    }else	{
                        $('#error-list-buyer').html(msg.msg);
                    }
                },
                error: function () {
                },
                complete: function () {
                    $('#success-message-buyer').html('<span>Your Message Has Been Sent Thank you!</span>');
                    setTimeout(function(){location.reload()}, 3000);
                }
            });
        }

        $('#hsc_country').change(function(){
            if($('#hsc_country').val() > 0)	{
                $('#hsc_country-error').hide();
            }
        });

        $('#hbc_country').change(function(){
            if($('#hbc_country').val() > 0)	{
                $('#hbc_country-error').hide();
                var selectedConValue = $(this).val();
                if(selectedConValue==48){
                    $('#BSbuyerConsultancyElement').show();
                    $('#CompbuyerConsultancyElement').show();
                }else{
                    $('#BSbuyerConsultancyElement').hide();
                    $('#CompbuyerConsultancyElement').hide();
                }

            }
        });

		$('.cookies').delay(20000).fadeOut('slow');
		
        $('.btn-cookies').click(function(){
            $('.cookies').hide();
            document.cookie = 'saveCookieStatus=cookiesaved; max-age=86400; path=/';
        });

    });

</script>

<script>
		function get_calling_code(country , form , id)
		{	
			if(country == "")
			{
				return;
			}
			$.ajax({
				type: "POST",
				url: "/signup/get_country_code",
				data: "country_id="+country,
				dataType: "html",
				beforeSend: function() {
					$("#county_loading_code").show();
				},
				complete: function() {
					$("#county_loading_code").hide();
				},
				success: function(msg)
				{
					$("#"+form+" #"+id).val("+"+msg);
				}
			});
		}
		</script>

<script type="text/javascript">							
				function verfiy_email_exit(email , forms , div)
				{
					if(email == "")
					{
						return;
					}

					$.ajax({
						type: "POST",
						url: "/tools/signup_verify_email",
						data: "email="+email,
						dataType: "json",
						success: function(msg)
						{	
							if(msg.msg != 1)
							{
								$("#"+forms+ " "+ "#"+div).text(msg.msg).show();
							}
							else if(msg.msg == 1)
							{
								$("#"+forms+ " "+ "#"+div).text("").hide();
							}
						}
					});	
				}


				
				document.addEventListener("mouseleave", function (e) {
                    if (e.clientY < 0) {
                        if (document.cookie.indexOf('e_id') == -1) {
                            $('#exit_intent').modal("show");
                            //$('#eh-auto-signup_popup').modal("hide");
                                $('#close_intent').click(function () {
                                    document.cookie = "e_id=1; expires=Thu, 10 Mar 2050 12:00:00 UTC,path=exporthub";
                                });
                        } 
                    }
                }, false);

                $('#exit_intent_form').bootstrapValidator({
                submitHandler: function () {

                    var data_filled = true;

                    if($("#set_is_buyer_seller_en").val()==2){
                        if($('#eicompany_field_inner').val()=='' || $('#eicompany_field_inner').val()==null){
                            $("#Error_span").show();
                            data_filled=false;
                        }else{
                            $("#Error_span").hide();
                            data_filled=true;
                        }
                    }

                    if(data_filled) {
                        $.ajax({
                            type: "POST",
                            url: "/tools/signup_verify_email",
                            data: $("#exit_intent_form").serialize(),
                            dataType: "json",
                            async: 1,
                            success: function (success) {
                                if (success.msg != 1) {
                                    $('#credentials_error_exixts_ei').show();
                                } else {
                                    $.ajax({
                                        type: "POST",
                                        url: "/signup/save_exit_intent_form",
                                        data: $("#exit_intent_form").serialize(),
                                        success: function (e) {
                                            if(e==1) {
                                                document.cookie = "e_id=1; expires=Thu, 10 Mar 2050 12:00:00 UTC,path=exporthub";
                                                $('#exit_intent').modal('hide');
                                                //$('').modal('show');
                                                $("#success_msg").fadeIn(1000, function () {
                                                    $(this).modal('show');
                                                    location.reload(true);
                                                });
                                            }
                                            else if(e==5)
                                            {
                                                //alert('ssss1002');
                                                $("#captcha_error_msg").fadeIn(1000, function () {
                                                    $(this).modal('show');
                                                });

                                                setTimeout(function() {
                                                    $('#captcha_error_msg').modal('hide');
                                                }, 3000);
                                            }
                                        }
                                    });

                                }
                            }
                        });
                    }
                },

                feedbackIcons: {
                   /* valid: 'fa fa-check',
                    invalid: 'fa fa-times',
                    validating: 'fa fa-refresh'*/
                },
                fields: {
                    name: {
                        validators: {
                            notEmpty: {
                                message: 'Please enter your name'
                            }
                        }
                    },
                    email: {
                        validators: {
                            notEmpty: {
                                message: 'Please enter your email address'
                            },
                            emailAddress: {
                                message: 'Please enter a valid email address'
                            }
                        }
                    },
                    country: {
                        validators: {
                            notEmpty: {
                                message: 'Please enter your country'
                            }
                        }
                    },
                    mobile1_c: {
                        validators: {
                            notEmpty: {
                                message: 'Enter code'
                            }
                        }
                    },
                    mobile: {
                        validators: {
                            notEmpty: {
                                message: 'Please enter mobile number'
                            }
                        }
                    },
                    selling_buying_products: {
                        validators: {
                            notEmpty: {
                                message: 'Please enter your company name'
                            }
                        }
                    },
                    captcha: {
                        validators: {
                            stringLength: {
                                min: 4,
                                max: 4,
                                message:'Please enter 4 characters'
                            },
                            notEmpty: {
                                message: 'Please enter captcha'
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            });
                $("#buyer_button_en").click(function () {
                    $("#set_is_buyer_seller_en").val(1);
                    $("#Error_span").hide();
                }),
                $("#seller_button_en").click(function () {
                    $("#set_is_buyer_seller_en").val(2);
                    if($('#eicompany_field_inner').val()=='' || $('#eicompany_field_inner').val()==null){
                        $("#Error_span").show();
                    }else{
                        $("#Error_span").hide();
                    }
                });
                $('#eicompany_field_inner').keyup(function () {
            if($('#eicompany_field_inner').val()!=''){
                $("#Error_span").hide();
            }else{
                $("#Error_span").show();
            }
            $('#seller_button_en').prop('disabled', false);
            $('#buyer_button_en').prop('disabled', false);
        })

<script>

    // email validation function
    function ValidateEmail(email){
        var re = /^(([^<>()\[\]\\.,;:\s@"]+(\.[^<>()\[\]\\.,;:\s@"]+)*)|(".+"))@((\[[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}])|(([a-zA-Z\-0-9]+\.)+[a-zA-Z]{2,}))$/;
        // alert(re.test(email));
        return re.test(email);
    }

    function view_member_info(source,page,heading)
    {
        //alert(source+' = '+page+" = "+heading);
        var site_id = '1';
        var login = '';


        if((site_id == 2|| site_id == 4) && (login == '') &&(getCookie('mem_info')) != 4 )
        {
            $('#success-message-member-info').hide();
            $('#members_info').show();
            $('#members_info_source').val(source);
            $('#member_info_heading').html(heading);
            $('#members_info_page_refer').val(page);
            $('#members_info_popup').modal('show');
        }
    }

    $(document).ready(function(){

        var site_id = '1';
        var login = '';

        if((site_id == 2 || site_id == 4) && (login == '') &&(getCookie('mem_info')) != 4 )	{
            $(".com-collapse-btn").click(function() {
                view_member_info('plus sign','responsive',' Provide Your Details to Access Full Details');
            });
        }
    });

    function getCookiesByName(cookiename)
    {
        var cookiestring=RegExp(""+cookiename+"[^;]+").exec(document.cookie);
        return decodeURIComponent(!!cookiestring ? cookiestring.toString().replace(/^[^=]+./,"") : "");
    }


    function set_close_mem_info(){
        var count_val = (getCookiesByName('mem_info') != "") ? parseInt(getCookiesByName('mem_info')) : parseInt(0);
        if(count_val < 3){
            setCookie('mem_info',parseInt(count_val)+1,30);
        }
        return true;
    }

    $("#members_info :submit").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        var form_data = $("#members_info");
        var data = form_data.serialize();
        errors=0;
        if($("#member_info_title").val() == '')
        {
            errors=1;
            document.getElementById("member_info_title").style.border="3px solid red";
        }
        else
        {
            document.getElementById("member_info_title").style.border="1px solid #ccc";
        }

        if($("#member_info_mobile").val() == '')
        {
            errors=1;
            document.getElementById("member_info_mobile").style.border="3px solid red";
        }
        else
        {
            document.getElementById("member_info_mobile").style.border="1px solid #ccc";
        }

        if($("#member_info_email").val() == '')
        {
            errors=1;
            document.getElementById("member_info_email").style.border="3px solid red";
        }
        else
        {
            var validate_email = ValidateEmail($("#member_info_email").val());
            if(validate_email){
                document.getElementById("member_info_email").style.border="1px solid #ccc";
            }else{
                errors=1;
                document.getElementById("member_info_email").style.border="3px solid red";
            }
        }

        if($("#member_info_company").val() == '')
        {
            errors=1;
            document.getElementById("member_info_company").style.border="3px solid red";
        }
        else
        {
            document.getElementById("member_info_company").style.border="1px solid #ccc";
        }

                $('#captcha-message-member-info').hide();
        if(errors == 1)
        {

            return false;
        }

        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            url: "/signup/send_members_info",
            data:data,
            success: function (get_data) {
                if(get_data!=5)
                {
                    $('#CaptchaErrorModal').modal('hide');
                    if (get_data=='11'){
                        $('#members_info').hide();
                        $('#success-message-member-info').show();
                        $('#success-message-member-info').html('注册成功！我们已经通过电子邮件发送了您的登录详细信息。验证电子邮件也已发送到您的电子邮件地址.');
                    }else if (get_data == '5'){
                        $('#captcha-message-member-info').show();
                        $('#captcha-message-member-info').html('验证码不正确');
                    }
                }
                else if(get_data==5)
                {
                    $('#CaptchaErrorModal').modal('show');
                    setTimeout(function() {
                        $('#CaptchaErrorModal').modal('hide');
                    }, 3000);
                }


            }
        });
    });

</script>
<script>
    $("#main_header_form :submit").click(function (e) {
        e.preventDefault();
        var form_data = $("#main_header_form");
        var data = form_data.serialize();
        errors=0;
        if($("#main_header_name").val() == '')
        {
            errors=1;
            document.getElementById("main_header_name").style.border="3px solid red";
        }
        else
        {
            document.getElementById("main_header_name").style.border="1px solid #ccc";
        }

        if($("#main_header_phone").val() == '')
        {
            errors=1;
            document.getElementById("main_header_phone").style.border="3px solid red";
        }
        else
        {
            document.getElementById("main_header_phone").style.border="1px solid #ccc";
        }

        if($("#main_header_email").val() == '')
        {
            errors=1;
            document.getElementById("main_header_email").style.border="3px solid red";
        }
        else
        {
            var validate_email = ValidateEmail($("#main_header_email").val());
            if(validate_email){
                document.getElementById("main_header_email").style.border="1px solid #ccc";
            }else{
                errors=1;
                document.getElementById("main_header_email").style.border="3px solid red";
            }
        }

        if($("#main_header_company").val() == '')
        {
            errors=1;
            document.getElementById("main_header_company").style.border="3px solid red";
        }
        else
        {
            document.getElementById("main_header_company").style.border="1px solid #ccc";
        }
        
        if(errors == 1)
        {
            return false;
        }
        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            url: "/signup/send_members_info",
            data:data,
            success: function (get_data) {
                if (get_data=='11'){
                    $('#form_div_header_bar').hide();
                    $('#success_msg_header_bar').show();
                    setTimeout(function() {
                        $('#success_msg_header_bar').fadeOut();
                    }, 5000);
                }else if(get_data=='4'){
                    $('#success_msg_header_bar').hide();
                    $('#error_msg_header_bar').show();
                    setTimeout(function() {
                        $('#error_msg_header_bar').fadeOut();
                    }, 5000);
                }else if(get_data=='5'){
                    $('#success_msg_header_bar').hide();
                    $('#error_msg_header_bar_captcha').show();
                    setTimeout(function() {
                        $('#error_msg_header_bar_captcha').fadeOut();
                    }, 5000);
                }
            }
        });

    });

    function claim_method()	{
        var form_data = $("#claim_company_form");
        var data = form_data.serialize();
        document.getElementById("error-list-supplier").innerHTML = "";

        errors=0;
        if($("#claim_mobile").val() == '')
        {
            errors=1;
            document.getElementById("claim_mobile").style.border="3px solid red";
        }
        else
        {
            document.getElementById("claim_mobile").style.border="1px solid #ccc";
        }

        if($("#claim_name").val() == '')
        {
            errors=1;
            document.getElementById("claim_name").style.border="3px solid red";
        }
        else
        {
            document.getElementById("claim_name").style.border="1px solid #ccc";
        }

        if($("#claim_email").val() == '')
        {
            errors=1;
            document.getElementById("claim_email").style.border="3px solid red";
        }
        else
        {
            var validate_email = ValidateEmail($("#claim_email").val());
            if(validate_email){
                document.getElementById("claim_email").style.border="1px solid #ccc";
            }else{
                errors=1;
                document.getElementById("claim_email").style.border="3px solid red";
            }
        }


        
        if(errors == 1)
        {
            return false;
        }
        $('#claim_submit_button').attr('disabled','disabled');
        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            url: "/claim_your_company",
            data:data,
            success: function (get_data) {
                if (get_data.data.status=='1'){
                    $('.error-list-claim').hide();
                    $('.success-message-claim').show();
                    setTimeout(function() {
                        $('.success-message-claim').fadeOut();
                        $('#claim_popup').modal('hide');
                    }, 5000);
                }else {
                    $('.success-message-claim').hide();
                    $('.error-list-claim').show();
                    $('.error-list-claim').html(get_data.data.message);
                    setTimeout(function() {
                        $('.error-list-claim').fadeOut();
                    }, 5000);
                }
                $('#claim_submit_button').removeAttr('disabled');
            }
        });
    }
	
	function new_header_image_signup()	{
		$('#eh-signup_popup-s1').modal('show');
		$('#eh_signUp_form input[name ="source"]').val('Sticky_Bar');
		$('#eh_signUp_form_s2').append('<input type="hidden" name="source" value="Sticky_Bar" />');
	}

<script>

    $(window).scroll(function(){
        var sticky = $('.rb_nav-ontop'),
            scroll = $(window).scrollTop();
        if (scroll >= 200)
        {
           sticky.addClass('rb_fixed');
        }
        else
        {
            sticky.removeClass('rb_fixed');
        }
    });

    function rb_drop() {
        document.getElementById("rb_myDropdown").classList.toggle("show");
    }

    window.onclick = function(event) {
        if (!event.target.matches('.rb_droper')) {
            var dropdowns = document.getElementsByClassName("rb_vertical-menu-content");
            var i;
            for (i = 0; i < dropdowns.length; i++) {
                var openDropdown = dropdowns[i];
                if (openDropdown.classList.contains('show')) {
                    openDropdown.classList.remove('show');
                }
            }
        }
    }
